<pr_description>
Wrong a11y wargning on <dialog> with autofocus attribute
### Describe the bug

Ally warning "Avoid using autofocus" appears on `<dialog autofocus>` element definition. 
But using of autofocus on dialog or its descendants is recommended by the standard: https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element

> As such, authors should use the [autofocus](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-fe-autofocus) attribute on the descendant element of the dialog that the user is expected to immediately interact with after the dialog opens. If there is no such element, then authors should use the [autofocus](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-fe-autofocus) attribute on the [dialog](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element) element itself.

### Reproduction

```html
<dialog autofocus>
	I'm a dialog
</dialog>
```

https://svelte.dev/repl/483135a2842e4da6ba6f24ea63430cf2?version=4.2.0

_No response_

```shell
N/A
```

annoyance

</pr_description>

    20	const aria_roles = roles_map.keys();
    21	const abstract_roles = aria_roles.filter((role) => roles_map.get(role)?.abstract);
    22	const non_abstract_roles = aria_roles.filter((name) => !abstract_roles.includes(name));
    23	const non_interactive_roles = non_abstract_roles
    24	        .filter((name) => {
    25	                const role = roles_map.get(name);
    26	                return (
    27	                        // 'toolbar' does not descend from widget, but it does support
    28	                        // aria-activedescendant, thus in practice we treat it as a widget.
    29	                        // focusable tabpanel elements are recommended if any panels in a set contain content where the first element in the panel is not focusable.
    30	                        // 'generic' is meant to have no semantic meaning.
    31	                        // 'cell' is treated as CellRole by the AXObject which is interactive, so we treat 'cell' it as interactive as well.
    32	                        !['toolbar', 'tabpanel', 'generic', 'cell'].includes(name) &&
    33	                        !role?.superClass.some((classes) => classes.includes('widget') || classes.includes('window'))
    34	                );
    35	        })
    36	        .concat(
    37	                // The `progressbar` is descended from `widget`, but in practice, its
    38	                // value is always `readonly`, so we treat it as a non-interactive role.
    39	                'progressbar'
    40	        );
    41	const interactive_roles = non_abstract_roles.filter(
    42	        (name) =>
    43	                !non_interactive_roles.includes(name) &&
    44	                // 'generic' is meant to have no semantic meaning.
    45	                name !== 'generic'
    46	);
    47

    49	 * @param {ARIARoleDefinitionKey} role

    51	function is_non_interactive_roles(role) {
    52	        return non_interactive_roles.includes(role);
    53	}

    56	 * @param {ARIARoleDefinitionKey} role

    58	function is_interactive_roles(role) {
    59	        return interactive_roles.includes(role);
    60	}

    66	        return abstract_roles.includes(role);

    78	/**
    79	 * @param {string} tag_name
    80	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
    81	 */
    82	function is_hidden_from_screen_reader(tag_name, attribute_map) {
    83	        if (tag_name === 'input') {
    84	                const type = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('type'));
    85	                if (type === 'hidden') {
    86	                        return true;
    87	                }
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        const aria_hidden = attribute_map.get('aria-hidden');
    91	        if (!aria_hidden) return false;
    92	        const aria_hidden_value = get_static_value(aria_hidden);
    93	        if (aria_hidden_value === null) return true;
    94	        return aria_hidden_value === true || aria_hidden_value === 'true';
    95	}
    96	
    97	/**
    98	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
    99	 */
   100	function has_disabled_attribute(attribute_map) {
   101	        const disabled_attr_value = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('disabled'));
   102	        if (disabled_attr_value) {
   103	                return true;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        const aria_disabled_attr = attribute_map.get('aria-disabled');
   107	        if (aria_disabled_attr) {
   108	                const aria_disabled_attr_value = get_static_value(aria_disabled_attr);
   109	                if (aria_disabled_attr_value === 'true') {
   110	                        return true;
   111	                }
   112	        }
   113	        return false;
   114	}

   117	 * @type {ARIARoleRelationConcept[]}

   119	const non_interactive_element_role_schemas = [];
   120	elementRoles.entries().forEach(([schema, roles]) => {
   121	        if ([...roles].every((role) => role !== 'generic' && non_interactive_roles.includes(role))) {
   122	                non_interactive_element_role_schemas.push(schema);
   123	        }

   129	const interactive_element_role_schemas = [];
   130	elementRoles.entries().forEach(([schema, roles]) => {
   131	        if ([...roles].every((role) => interactive_roles.includes(role))) {
   132	                interactive_element_role_schemas.push(schema);
   133	        }

   135	const interactive_ax_objects = [...AXObjects.keys()].filter(
   136	        (name) => AXObjects.get(name).type === 'widget'

   139	        ['windows', 'structure'].includes(AXObjects.get(name).type)

   153	                }
   154	        }

   161	elementAXObjects.entries().forEach(
   162	        /**
   163	         * @param {any} _
   164	         */
   165	        ([schema, ax_object]) => {
   166	                if ([...ax_object].every((role) => non_interactive_ax_objects.includes(role))) {
   167	                        non_interactive_element_ax_object_schemas.push(schema);
   168	                }
   169	        }
   170	);

   172	/**
   173	 * @param {ARIARoleRelationConcept} schema
   174	 * @param {string} tag_name
   175	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
   176	 */
   177	function match_schema(schema, tag_name, attribute_map) {
   178	        if (schema.name !== tag_name) return false;
   179	        if (!schema.attributes) return true;
   180	        return schema.attributes.every((schema_attribute) => {
   181	                const attribute = attribute_map.get(schema_attribute.name);
   182	                if (!attribute) return false;
   183	                if (schema_attribute.value && schema_attribute.value !== get_static_text_value(attribute)) {
   184	                        return false;
   185	                }
   186	                return true;
   187	        });
   188	}
   189	
   190	const ElementInteractivity = /** @type {const} */ ({
   191	        Interactive: 'interactive',
   192	        NonInteractive: 'non-interactive',
   193	        Static: 'static'
   194	});
   195	
   196	/**
   197	 * @param {string} tag_name
   198	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
   199	 * @returns {ElementInteractivity[keyof ElementInteractivity]}
   200	 */
   201	function element_interactivity(tag_name, attribute_map) {
   202	        if (
   203	                interactive_element_role_schemas.some((schema) => match_schema(schema, tag_name, attribute_map))
   204	        ) {
   205	                return ElementInteractivity.Interactive;
   206	        }
   207	        if (
   208	                tag_name !== 'header' &&
   209	                non_interactive_element_role_schemas.some((schema) =>
   210	                        match_schema(schema, tag_name, attribute_map)
   211	                )
   212	        ) {
   213	                return ElementInteractivity.NonInteractive;
   214	        }
   215	        if (
   216	                interactive_element_ax_object_schemas.some((schema) =>
   217	                        match_schema(schema, tag_name, attribute_map)
   218	                )
   219	        ) {
   220	                return ElementInteractivity.Interactive;
   221	        }
   222	        if (
   223	                non_interactive_element_ax_object_schemas.some((schema) =>
   224	                        match_schema(schema, tag_name, attribute_map)
   225	                )
   226	        ) {
   227	                return ElementInteractivity.NonInteractive;
   228	        }
   229	        return ElementInteractivity.Static;
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 * @param {string} tag_name
   234	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
   235	 * @returns {boolean}
   236	 */
   237	function is_interactive_element(tag_name, attribute_map) {
   238	        return element_interactivity(tag_name, attribute_map) === ElementInteractivity.Interactive;
   239	}
   240	
   241	/**
   242	 * @param {string} tag_name
   243	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
   244	 * @returns {boolean}
   245	 */
   246	function is_non_interactive_element(tag_name, attribute_map) {
   247	        return element_interactivity(tag_name, attribute_map) === ElementInteractivity.NonInteractive;
   248	}

   255	function is_static_element(tag_name, attribute_map) {

   257	}

   263	 */
   264	function is_semantic_role_element(role, tag_name, attribute_map) {
   265	        for (const [schema, ax_object] of elementAXObjects.entries()) {
   266	                if (
   267	                        schema.name === tag_name &&
   268	                        (!schema.attributes ||
   269	                                schema.attributes.every(
   270	                                        /** @param {any} attr */
   271	                                        (attr) =>
   272	                                                attribute_map.has(attr.name) &&
   273	                                                get_static_value(attribute_map.get(attr.name)) === attr.value
   274	                                ))
   275	                ) {
   276	                        for (const name of ax_object) {
   277	                                const roles = AXObjectRoles.get(name);
   278	                                if (roles) {
   279	                                        for (const { name } of roles) {
   280	                                                if (name === role) {
   281	                                                        return true;
   282	                                                }
   283	                                        }
   284	                                }
   285	                        }
   286	                }
   287	        }
   288	        return false;
   289	}

   356	/**
   357	 * @param {null | true | string} autocomplete
   358	 */
   359	function is_valid_autocomplete(autocomplete) {
   360	        if (autocomplete === true) {
   361	                return false;
   362	        } else if (!autocomplete) {
   363	                return true; // dynamic value
   364	        }
   365	        const tokens = autocomplete.trim().toLowerCase().split(regex_whitespaces);
   366	        if (typeof tokens[0] === 'string' && tokens[0].startsWith('section-')) {
   367	                tokens.shift();
   368	        }
   369	        if (address_type_tokens.includes(tokens[0])) {
   370	                tokens.shift();
   371	        }
   372	        if (autofill_field_name_tokens.includes(tokens[0])) {
   373	                tokens.shift();
   374	        } else {
   375	                if (contact_type_tokens.includes(tokens[0])) {
   376	                        tokens.shift();
   377	                }
   378	                if (autofill_contact_field_name_tokens.includes(tokens[0])) {
   379	                        tokens.shift();
   380	                } else {
   381	                        return false;
   382	                }
   383	        }
   384	        if (tokens[0] === 'webauthn') {
   385	                tokens.shift();
   386	        }
   387	        return tokens.length === 0;
   388	}

   544	const combobox_if_list = ['email', 'search', 'tel', 'text', 'url'];
   545	
   546	/** @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map */
   547	function input_implicit_role(attribute_map) {
   548	        const type_attribute = attribute_map.get('type');
   549	        if (!type_attribute) return;
   550	        const type = get_static_text_value(type_attribute);
   551	        if (!type) return;
   552	        const list_attribute_exists = attribute_map.has('list');
   553	        if (list_attribute_exists && combobox_if_list.includes(type)) {
   554	                return 'combobox';
   555	        }
   556	        return input_type_to_implicit_role.get(type);
   557	}
   558	
   559	/** @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map */
   560	function menuitem_implicit_role(attribute_map) {
   561	        const type_attribute = attribute_map.get('type');
   562	        if (!type_attribute) return;
   563	        const type = get_static_text_value(type_attribute);
   564	        if (!type) return;
   565	        return menuitem_type_to_implicit_role.get(type);
   566	}
   567	
   568	/**
   569	 * @param {string} name
   570	 * @param {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} attribute_map
   571	 */
   572	function get_implicit_role(name, attribute_map) {
   573	        if (name === 'menuitem') {
   574	                return menuitem_implicit_role(attribute_map);
   575	        } else if (name === 'input') {
   576	                return input_implicit_role(attribute_map);
   577	        } else {
   578	                return a11y_implicit_semantics.get(name);
   579	        }
   580	}

   582	const invisible_elements = ['meta', 'html', 'script', 'style'];
   583	
   584	/**
   585	 * @param {AST.SvelteNode[]} path
   586	 * @param {string[]} elements
   587	 */
   588	function is_parent(path, elements) {
   589	        let i = path.length;
   590	        while (i--) {
   591	                const parent = path[i];
   592	                if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
   593	                if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
   594	                        return elements.includes(parent.name);
   595	                }
   596	        }
   597	        return false;
   598	}

   584	/**
   585	 * @param {AST.SvelteNode[]} path
   586	 * @param {string[]} elements
   587	 */
   588	function is_parent(path, elements) {
   589	        let i = path.length;
   590	        while (i--) {
   591	                const parent = path[i];
   592	                if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
   593	                if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
   594	                        return elements.includes(parent.name);
   595	                }
   596	        }
   597	        return false;
   598	}

```javascript
        if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
        if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
            return elements.includes(parent.name);
        }
    }
    return false;
}
```

```javascript
function is_parent(path, elements) {
```

OBSERVATION:

function is_parent(path, elements) {
	let i = path.length;
	while (i--) {
		const parent = path[i];
		if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
		if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
			return elements.includes(parent.name);
		}
	}
	return false;
}

So `is_parent` is used for:
1. Checking if header/footer is a child of section/article (should check ancestors)
2. Checking if autofocus is inside a dialog (should check ancestors)
3. Checking if figcaption is an immediate child of figure (should check immediate parent only!)

So we have two different behaviors needed. Let me look at the original function's behavior again. Looking at it more carefully:

```javascript
function is_parent(path, elements) {
    let i = path.length;
    while (i--) {
        const parent = path[i];
        if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
        if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
            return elements.includes(parent.name);
        }
    }
    return false;
}
```

This function returns as soon as it finds a RegularElement. So it checks **only the immediate parent** that is a RegularElement (ignoring Fragment nodes etc). So for the header/footer case, it's checking the immediate parent.

The problem is that the original function checks only the **immediate RegularElement parent**, while what we need for dialog/autofocus is to check **any RegularElement ancestor**. 

Actually, wait. Let me re-read the original function more carefully:

```javascript
function is_parent(path, elements) {
    let i = path.length;
    while (i--) {  // going backwards from the end
        const parent = path[i];
        if (parent.type === 'SvelteElement') return true; // unknown, play it safe, so we don't warn
        if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
            return elements.includes(parent.name);  // returns true or false and stops
        }
    }
    return false;
}
```

So it goes backward through the path and returns **as soon as it finds a RegularElement**. This means it checks the **first RegularElement it finds going backward**, which would be the immediate parent (assuming the path doesn't include the current node itself).

Now, looking at the figcaption test case:

When checking the `figcaption`, the path would be: `[..., figure, div]` (going from root to immediate parent).

When we iterate backward with `while (i--)`, we start from `div` (the immediate parent). The original function returns `elements.includes('div')` which is `false` for `['figure']`, so the warning is correctly triggered.

With our modification, we continue iterating and find `figure`, which returns `true`, so no warning is triggered - which is wrong!

function test(name, code, expectWarning) {
    const result = compile(code, { generate: false });
    const hasWarning = result.warnings.some(w => w.code === '"'"'a11y_autofocus'"'"');

    }
    return hasWarning === expectWarning;
}

-	// Check content
-	if (
-		!has_spread &&

-		a11y_required_content.includes(node.name) &&

-		w.a11y_missing_content(node, node.name);

+        /** @type {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} */
+        const attribute_map = new Map();
+
+        /** @type {Set<string>} */
+        const handlers = new Set();
+
+        /** @type {AST.Attribute[]} */
+        const attributes = [];
+
+        const is_dynamic_element = node.type === 'SvelteElement';
+
+        let has_spread = false;
+        let has_contenteditable_attr = false;
+        let has_contenteditable_binding = false;
+
+        for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
+                if (attribute.type === 'SpreadAttribute') {
+                        has_spread = true;
+                } else if (attribute.type === 'OnDirective') {
+                        handlers.add(attribute.name);
+                } else if (attribute.type === 'Attribute') {
+                        if (is_event_attribute(attribute)) {
+                                handlers.add(attribute.name.slice(2));
+                        } else {
+                                attributes.push(attribute);
+                                attribute_map.set(attribute.name, attribute);
+                                if (attribute.name === 'contenteditable') {
+                                        has_contenteditable_attr = true;
+                                }
+                        }
+                } else if (attribute.type === 'BindDirective' && is_content_editable_binding(attribute.name)) {
+                        has_contenteditable_binding = true;
+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
+                if (attribute.type !== 'Attribute') continue;
+
+                const name = attribute.name.toLowerCase();
+                // aria-props
+                if (name.startsWith('aria-')) {
+                        if (invisible_elements.includes(node.name)) {
+                                // aria-unsupported-elements
+                                w.a11y_aria_attributes(attribute, node.name);
+                        }
+
+                        const type = name.slice(5);
+                        if (!aria_attributes.includes(type)) {
+                                const match = fuzzymatch(type, aria_attributes);
+                                w.a11y_unknown_aria_attribute(attribute, type, match);
+                        }
+
+                        if (name === 'aria-hidden' && regex_heading_tags.test(node.name)) {
+                                w.a11y_hidden(attribute, node.name);
+                        }
+
+                        // aria-proptypes
+                        let value = get_static_value(attribute);
+
+                        const schema = aria.get(/** @type {ARIAProperty} */ (name));
+                        if (schema !== undefined) {
+                                validate_aria_attribute_value(attribute, /** @type {ARIAProperty} */ (name), schema, value);
+                        }
+
+                        // aria-activedescendant-has-tabindex
+                        if (
+                                name === 'aria-activedescendant' &&
+                                !is_dynamic_element &&
+                                !is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                !attribute_map.has('tabindex') &&
+                                !has_spread
+                        ) {
+                                w.a11y_aria_activedescendant_has_tabindex(attribute);
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // aria-role
+                if (name === 'role') {
+                        if (invisible_elements.includes(node.name)) {
+                                // aria-unsupported-elements
+                                w.a11y_misplaced_role(attribute, node.name);
+                        }
+
+                        const value = get_static_value(attribute);
+                        if (typeof value === 'string') {
+                                for (const c_r of value.split(regex_whitespaces)) {
+                                        const current_role = /** @type {ARIARoleDefinitionKey} current_role */ (c_r);
+
+                                        if (current_role && is_abstract_role(current_role)) {
+                                                w.a11y_no_abstract_role(attribute, current_role);
+                                        } else if (current_role && !aria_roles.includes(current_role)) {
+                                                const match = fuzzymatch(current_role, aria_roles);
+                                                w.a11y_unknown_role(attribute, current_role, match);
+                                        }
+
+                                        // no-redundant-roles
+                                        if (
+                                                current_role === get_implicit_role(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                                // <ul role="list"> is ok because CSS list-style:none removes the semantics and this is a way to bring them back
+                                                !['ul', 'ol', 'li'].includes(node.name) &&
+                                                // <a role="link" /> is ok because without href the a tag doesn't have a role of link
+                                                !(node.name === 'a' && !attribute_map.has('href'))
+                                        ) {
+                                                w.a11y_no_redundant_roles(attribute, current_role);
+                                        }
+
+                                        // Footers and headers are special cases, and should not have redundant roles unless they are the children of sections or articles.
+                                        const is_parent_section_or_article = is_parent(context.path, ['section', 'article']);
+                                        if (!is_parent_section_or_article) {
+                                                const has_nested_redundant_role =
+                                                        current_role === a11y_nested_implicit_semantics.get(node.name);
+                                                if (has_nested_redundant_role) {
+                                                        w.a11y_no_redundant_roles(attribute, current_role);
+                                                }
+                                        }
+
+                                        // role-has-required-aria-props
+                                        if (
+                                                !is_dynamic_element &&
+                                                !is_semantic_role_element(current_role, node.name, attribute_map)
+                                        ) {
+                                                const role = roles_map.get(current_role);
+                                                if (role) {
+                                                        const required_role_props = Object.keys(role.requiredProps);
+                                                        const has_missing_props =
+                                                                !has_spread &&
+                                                                required_role_props.some((prop) => !attributes.find((a) => a.name === prop));
+                                                        if (has_missing_props) {
+                                                                w.a11y_role_has_required_aria_props(
+                                                                        attribute,
+                                                                        current_role,
+                                                                        list(
+                                                                                required_role_props.map((v) => `"${v}"`),
+                                                                                'and'
+                                                                        )
+                                                                );
+                                                        }
+                                                }
+                                        }
+
+                                        // interactive-supports-focus
+                                        if (
+                                                !has_spread &&
+                                                !has_disabled_attribute(attribute_map) &&
+                                                !is_hidden_from_screen_reader(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                                !is_presentation_role(current_role) &&
+                                                is_interactive_roles(current_role) &&
+                                                is_static_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                                !attribute_map.get('tabindex')
+                                        ) {
+                                                const has_interactive_handlers = [...handlers].some((handler) =>
+                                                        a11y_interactive_handlers.includes(handler)
+                                                );
+                                                if (has_interactive_handlers) {
+                                                        w.a11y_interactive_supports_focus(node, current_role);
+                                                }
+                                        }
+
+                                        // no-interactive-element-to-noninteractive-role
+                                        if (
+                                                !has_spread &&
+                                                is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                                (is_non_interactive_roles(current_role) || is_presentation_role(current_role))
+                                        ) {
+                                                w.a11y_no_interactive_element_to_noninteractive_role(node, node.name, current_role);
+                                        }
+
+                                        // no-noninteractive-element-to-interactive-role
+                                        if (
+                                                !has_spread &&
+                                                is_non_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                                                is_interactive_roles(current_role) &&
+                                                !a11y_non_interactive_element_to_interactive_role_exceptions[node.name]?.includes(
+                                                        current_role
+                                                )
+                                        ) {
+                                                w.a11y_no_noninteractive_element_to_interactive_role(node, node.name, current_role);
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // no-access-key
+                if (name === 'accesskey') {
+                        w.a11y_accesskey(attribute);
+                }
+
+                // no-autofocus
+                if (name === 'autofocus' && !is_dynamic_element && node.name !== 'dialog' && !has_ancestor(context.path, ['dialog'])) {
+                        w.a11y_autofocus(attribute);
+                }
+
+                // scope
+                if (name === 'scope' && !is_dynamic_element && node.name !== 'th') {
+                        w.a11y_misplaced_scope(attribute);
+                }
+
+                // tabindex-no-positive
+                if (name === 'tabindex') {
+                        const value = get_static_value(attribute);
+                        // @ts-ignore todo is tabindex=true correct case?
+                        if (!isNaN(value) && +value > 0) {
+                                w.a11y_positive_tabindex(attribute);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        const role = attribute_map.get('role');
+        const role_static_value = /** @type {ARIARoleDefinitionKey} */ (get_static_text_value(role));
+
+        // click-events-have-key-events
+        if (handlers.has('click')) {
+                const is_non_presentation_role =
+                        role_static_value !== null && !is_presentation_role(role_static_value);
+                if (
+                        !is_dynamic_element &&
+                        !is_hidden_from_screen_reader(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                        (!role || is_non_presentation_role) &&
+                        !is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                        !has_spread
+                ) {
+                        const has_key_event =
+                                handlers.has('keydown') || handlers.has('keyup') || handlers.has('keypress');
+                        if (!has_key_event) {
+                                w.a11y_click_events_have_key_events(node);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        const role_value = /** @type {ARIARoleDefinitionKey} */ (
+                role ? role_static_value : get_implicit_role(node.name, attribute_map)
+        );
+
+        // no-noninteractive-tabindex
+        if (
+                !is_dynamic_element &&
+                !is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                !is_interactive_roles(role_static_value)
+        ) {
+                const tab_index = attribute_map.get('tabindex');
+                const tab_index_value = get_static_text_value(tab_index);
+                if (tab_index && (tab_index_value === null || Number(tab_index_value) >= 0)) {
+                        w.a11y_no_noninteractive_tabindex(node);
+                }
+        }
+
+        // role-supports-aria-props
+        if (typeof role_value === 'string' && roles_map.has(role_value)) {
+                const { props } = /** @type {ARIARoleDefinition} */ (roles_map.get(role_value));
+                const invalid_aria_props = aria.keys().filter((attribute) => !(attribute in props));
+                const is_implicit = role_value && role === undefined;
+                for (const attr of attributes) {
+                        if (invalid_aria_props.includes(/** @type {ARIAProperty} */ (attr.name))) {
+                                if (is_implicit) {
+                                        w.a11y_role_supports_aria_props_implicit(attr, attr.name, role_value, node.name);
+                                } else {
+                                        w.a11y_role_supports_aria_props(attr, attr.name, role_value);
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        // no-noninteractive-element-interactions
+        if (
+                !has_spread &&
+                !has_contenteditable_attr &&
+                !is_hidden_from_screen_reader(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                !is_presentation_role(role_static_value) &&
+                ((!is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                        is_non_interactive_roles(role_static_value)) ||
+                        (is_non_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) && !role))
+        ) {
+                const has_interactive_handlers = [...handlers].some((handler) =>
+                        a11y_recommended_interactive_handlers.includes(handler)
+                );
+                if (has_interactive_handlers) {
+                        w.a11y_no_noninteractive_element_interactions(node, node.name);
+                }
+        }
+
+        // no-static-element-interactions
+        if (
+                !has_spread &&
+                (!role || role_static_value !== null) &&
+                !is_hidden_from_screen_reader(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                !is_presentation_role(role_static_value) &&
+                !is_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                !is_interactive_roles(role_static_value) &&
+                !is_non_interactive_element(node.name, attribute_map) &&
+                !is_non_interactive_roles(role_static_value) &&
+                !is_abstract_role(role_static_value)
+        ) {
+                const interactive_handlers = [...handlers].filter((handler) =>
+                        a11y_interactive_handlers.includes(handler)
+                );
+                if (interactive_handlers.length > 0) {
+                        w.a11y_no_static_element_interactions(node, node.name, list(interactive_handlers));
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (!has_spread && handlers.has('mouseover') && !handlers.has('focus')) {
+                w.a11y_mouse_events_have_key_events(node, 'mouseover', 'focus');
+        }
+
+        if (!has_spread && handlers.has('mouseout') && !handlers.has('blur')) {
+                w.a11y_mouse_events_have_key_events(node, 'mouseout', 'blur');
+        }
+
+        // element-specific checks
+        const is_labelled = attribute_map.has('aria-label') || attribute_map.has('aria-labelledby');
+
+        if (node.name === 'a' || node.name === 'button') {
+                const is_hidden = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('aria-hidden')) === 'true';
+
+                if (!has_spread && !is_hidden && !is_labelled && !has_content(node)) {
+                        w.a11y_consider_explicit_label(node);
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'a') {
+                const href = attribute_map.get('href') || attribute_map.get('xlink:href');
+                if (href) {
+                        const href_value = get_static_text_value(href);
+                        if (href_value !== null) {
+                                if (href_value === '' || href_value === '#' || /^\W*javascript:/i.test(href_value)) {
+                                        w.a11y_invalid_attribute(href, href_value, href.name);
+                                }
+                        }
+                } else if (!has_spread) {
+                        const id_attribute = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('id'));
+                        const name_attribute = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('name'));
+                        const aria_disabled_attribute = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('aria-disabled'));
+                        if (!id_attribute && !name_attribute && aria_disabled_attribute !== 'true') {
+                                warn_missing_attribute(node, ['href']);
+                        }
+                }
+        } else if (!has_spread) {
+                const required_attributes = a11y_required_attributes[node.name];
+                if (required_attributes) {
+                        const has_attribute = required_attributes.some((name) => attribute_map.has(name));
+                        if (!has_attribute) {
+                                warn_missing_attribute(node, required_attributes);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'input') {
+                const type = attribute_map.get('type');
+                const type_value = get_static_text_value(type);
+                if (type_value === 'image' && !has_spread) {
+                        const required_attributes = ['alt', 'aria-label', 'aria-labelledby'];
+                        const has_attribute = required_attributes.some((name) => attribute_map.has(name));
+                        if (!has_attribute) {
+                                warn_missing_attribute(node, required_attributes, 'input type="image"');
+                        }
+                }
+                // autocomplete-valid
+                const autocomplete = attribute_map.get('autocomplete');
+                if (type && autocomplete) {
+                        const autocomplete_value = get_static_value(autocomplete);
+                        if (!is_valid_autocomplete(autocomplete_value)) {
+                                w.a11y_autocomplete_valid(
+                                        autocomplete,
+                                        /** @type {string} */ (autocomplete_value),
+                                        type_value ?? '...'
+                                );
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'img') {
+                const alt_attribute = get_static_text_value(attribute_map.get('alt'));
+                const aria_hidden = get_static_value(attribute_map.get('aria-hidden'));
+                if (alt_attribute && !aria_hidden && !has_spread) {
+                        if (/\b(image|picture|photo)\b/i.test(alt_attribute)) {
+                                w.a11y_img_redundant_alt(node);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'label') {
+                /** @param {AST.TemplateNode} node */
+                const has_input_child = (node) => {
+                        let has = false;
+                        walk(
+                                node,
+                                {},
+                                {
+                                        _(node, { next }) {
+                                                if (
+                                                        node.type === 'SvelteElement' ||
+                                                        node.type === 'SlotElement' ||
+                                                        node.type === 'Component' ||
+                                                        node.type === 'RenderTag' ||
+                                                        (node.type === 'RegularElement' &&
+                                                                (a11y_labelable.includes(node.name) || node.name === 'slot'))
+                                                ) {
+                                                        has = true;
+                                                } else {
+                                                        next();
+                                                }
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        );
+                        return has;
+                };
+                if (!has_spread && !attribute_map.has('for') && !has_input_child(node)) {
+                        w.a11y_label_has_associated_control(node);
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'video') {
+                const aria_hidden_attribute = attribute_map.get('aria-hidden');
+                const aria_hidden_exist = aria_hidden_attribute && get_static_value(aria_hidden_attribute);
+                if (attribute_map.has('muted') || aria_hidden_exist === 'true' || has_spread) {
+                        return;
+                }
+                let has_caption = false;
+                const track = /** @type {AST.RegularElement | undefined} */ (
+                        node.fragment.nodes.find((i) => i.type === 'RegularElement' && i.name === 'track')
+                );
+                if (track) {
+                        has_caption = track.attributes.some(
+                                (a) =>
+                                        a.type === 'SpreadAttribute' ||
+                                        (a.type === 'Attribute' && a.name === 'kind' && get_static_value(a) === 'captions')
+                        );
+                }
+                if (!has_caption) {
+                        w.a11y_media_has_caption(node);
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'figcaption') {
+                if (!is_parent(context.path, ['figure'])) {
+                        w.a11y_figcaption_parent(node);
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (node.name === 'figure') {
+                const children = node.fragment.nodes.filter((node) => {
+                        if (node.type === 'Comment') return false;
+                        if (node.type === 'Text') return regex_not_whitespace.test(node.data);
+                        return true;
+                });
+                const index = children.findIndex(
+                        (child) => child.type === 'RegularElement' && child.name === 'figcaption'
+                );
+                if (index !== -1 && index !== 0 && index !== children.length - 1) {
+                        w.a11y_figcaption_index(children[index]);
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (a11y_distracting_elements.includes(node.name)) {
+                // no-distracting-elements
+                w.a11y_distracting_elements(node, node.name);
+        }
+
+        // Check content
+        if (
+                !has_spread &&
+                !is_labelled &&
+                !has_contenteditable_binding &&
+                a11y_required_content.includes(node.name) &&
+                !has_content(node)
+        ) {
+                w.a11y_missing_content(node, node.name);
+        }
 }
 
 /**
  * @param {AST.RegularElement | AST.SvelteElement} element
  */
 function has_content(element) {
-	for (const node of element.fragment.nodes) {
-		if (node.type === 'Text') {
-			if (node.data.trim() === '') {
-				continue;
-			}
-		}
-
-		if (node.type === 'RegularElement' || node.type === 'SvelteElement') {
-			if (
-				node.name === 'img' &&
-				node.attributes.some((node) => node.type === 'Attribute' && node.name === 'alt')
-			) {
-				return true;
-			}
-
-			if (!has_content(node)) {
-				continue;
-			}
-		}
-
-		// assume everything else has content — this will result in false positives
-		// (e.g. an empty `{#if ...}{/if}`) but that's probably fine
-		return true;
-	}
+        for (const node of element.fragment.nodes) {
+                if (node.type === 'Text') {
+                        if (node.data.trim() === '') {
+                                continue;
+                        }
+                }
+
+                if (node.type === 'RegularElement' || node.type === 'SvelteElement') {
+                        if (
+                                node.name === 'img' &&
+                                node.attributes.some((node) => node.type === 'Attribute' && node.name === 'alt')
+                        ) {
+                                return true;
+                        }
+
+                        if (!has_content(node)) {
+                                continue;
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // assume everything else has content — this will result in false positives
+                // (e.g. an empty `{#if ...}{/if}`) but that's probably fine
+                return true;
+        }
 }

diff --git a/test_comprehensive.js b/test_comprehensive.js
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..180bd8080
--- /dev/null
+++ b/test_comprehensive.js
@@ -0,0 +1,45 @@
+import { compile } from './packages/svelte/src/compiler/index.js';
+
+function test(name, code, expectWarning) {
+    const result = compile(code, { generate: false });
+    const hasWarning = result.warnings.some(w => w.code === 'a11y_autofocus');
+    const status = hasWarning === expectWarning ? '✓' : '✗';
+    console.log(`${status} ${name}`);
+    if (hasWarning !== expectWarning) {
+        console.log(`  Expected: ${expectWarning ? 'warning' : 'no warning'}, Got: ${hasWarning ? 'warning' : 'no warning'}`);
+        console.log(`  Code: ${code.replace(/\n/g, ' ')}`);
+    }
+    return hasWarning === expectWarning;
+}
+
+console.log('Testing autofocus a11y warnings with dialog elements:\n');
+
+let passed = 0;
+let failed = 0;
+
+// Should NOT warn
+if (test('dialog with autofocus', `<dialog autofocus></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input inside dialog', `<dialog><input autofocus /></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('button inside dialog', `<dialog><button autofocus>OK</button></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('textarea inside dialog', `<dialog><textarea autofocus></textarea></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('select inside dialog', `<dialog><select autofocus><option>1</option></select></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('deeply nested input in dialog', `<dialog><div><div><input autofocus /></div></div></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input in form in dialog', `<dialog><form><input autofocus /></form></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+
+// Should warn
+if (test('div with autofocus', `<div autofocus></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input with autofocus', `<input autofocus />`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('button with autofocus', `<button autofocus>Click</button>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input in div', `<div><input autofocus /></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input after dialog', `<dialog></dialog><input autofocus />`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input before dialog', `<input autofocus /><dialog></dialog>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input in sibling of dialog', `<div><dialog></dialog><input autofocus /></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+
+console.log(`\nResults: ${passed}/${passed+failed} tests passed`);
+
+if (failed > 0) {
+    console.log(`\n❌ ${failed} test(s) failed`);
+    process.exit(1);
+} else {
+    console.log('\n✅ All tests passed!');
+}

+import { compile } from './packages/svelte/src/compiler/index.js';
+
+function test(name, code, expectWarning) {
+    console.log(`Test: ${name}`);
+    console.log(`Code: ${code}`);
+    const result = compile(code, { generate: false });
+    const hasWarning = result.warnings.some(w => w.code === 'a11y_autofocus');
+    const status = hasWarning === expectWarning ? '✓ PASS' : '✗ FAIL';
+    console.log(`Expected warning: ${expectWarning}, Got warning: ${hasWarning} - ${status}`);
+    if (hasWarning !== expectWarning) {
+        console.log('Warnings:', result.warnings.map(w => ({ code: w.code, message: w.message })));
+    }
+    console.log();
+    return hasWarning === expectWarning;
+}
+
+let passed = 0;
+let failed = 0;
+
+// Test cases
+if (test('div with autofocus', `<div autofocus></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('dialog with autofocus', `<dialog autofocus></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input inside dialog with autofocus', `<dialog><input autofocus></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input outside dialog with autofocus', `<div><input autofocus></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('button with autofocus', `<button autofocus>Click</button>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('button inside dialog with autofocus', `<dialog><button autofocus>Click</button></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('nested input inside dialog', `<dialog><div><input autofocus></div></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('nested input outside dialog', `<div><div><input autofocus></div></div>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('multiple dialogs nested', `<dialog><dialog><input autofocus></dialog></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('input after dialog', `<dialog></dialog><input autofocus>`, true)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('select inside dialog', `<dialog><select autofocus><option>1</option></select></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+if (test('textarea inside dialog', `<dialog><textarea autofocus></textarea></dialog>`, false)) passed++; else failed++;
+
+console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(50));
+console.log(`Results: ${passed} passed, ${failed} failed`);
+console.log('='.repeat(50));

+import { compile } from './packages/svelte/src/compiler/index.js';
+
+function test(name, code, expectWarning) {
+    const result = compile(code, { generate: false });
+    const hasWarning = result.warnings.some(w => w.code === 'a11y_autofocus');
+    const status = hasWarning === expectWarning ? '✓' : '✗';
+    console.log(`${status} ${name}`);
+    if (hasWarning !== expectWarning) {
+        console.log(`  Expected: ${expectWarning ? 'warning' : 'no warning'}, Got: ${hasWarning ? 'warning' : 'no warning'}`);
+    }
+    return hasWarning === expectWarning;
+}
+
+console.log('Testing SvelteElement edge cases:\n');
+
+// Test with dynamic elements (SvelteElement)
+test('dynamic element with autofocus', `<svelte:element this="div" autofocus />`, false);  // Should not warn (unknown element type)
+test('input in dynamic element', `<svelte:element this="div"><input autofocus /></svelte:element>`, false);  // Should not warn
+
+console.log('\nTesting nested dialogs:\n');
+
+test('nested dialogs', `<dialog><dialog><input autofocus /></dialog></dialog>`, false);
+test('dialog in article in dialog', `<dialog><article><dialog><input autofocus /></dialog></article></dialog>`, false);
+
+console.log('\nTesting other elements that might be confused:\n');
+
+// These should all warn (not dialog)
+test('details with autofocus', `<details autofocus></details>`, true);
+test('input in details', `<details><input autofocus /></details>`, true);
+test('datalist with autofocus', `<datalist autofocus></datalist>`, true);
